type of process or operation it represents. For example, an execution artifact represents a file that was processed, a fragment artifact represents a part of a larger transaction, and a fault artifact represents an error that occurred during processing.</p><div><section class="rounded-md border bg-fd-card"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between p-3 border-t border-b first:border-t-0 last:rounded-b-md first:rounded-t-md"><div <p>A partnership describes all aspects of the EDI relationship between two profiles in your Stedi account, such as which transaction sets they will exchange and other important information for processing EDI files. If you&#x27;re sending or receiving transactions through the Stedi clearinghouse, Stedi configures the necessary partnership for you automatically when you set up your account.</p><details
